A1: @DeptofDefense uses the DES to evaluate and return to duty, separate or retire Service members due to medical disability. DoD compensates medically separated or retired Service members for injuries or illness incurred or aggravated in the line of duty. #DESTalks https://t.co/oGIO5y3dUU
Thanks for following the #DESTalks Twitter chat! For more information on the disability evaluation system, visit: https://t.co/4XnNZnW4jJ https://t.co/SDoNd5KOZe
A8: The Physical Evaluation Board determines the fitness of Service members with medical conditions to perform their military duties. #DESTalks https://t.co/W0zdxVTOPq
Q8:  Who determines if a Service member can continue their military service (i.e., is fit for duty)? #DESTalks https://t.co/Z1QfPXn3BL
A7:  The Medical Evaluation Board determines whether a Service member's medical condition(s) prevent them from meeting their Service's medical retention standards. #DESTalks https://t.co/QktHF6Ksbh
Q7: Who determines if a Service member meets medical retention standards? #DESTalks https://t.co/28vCxA6jVl
A6: Service members in a valid duty status who incur or aggravate a medical condition in the line of duty. This includes:	- Reserve members on IDT orders	- Cadets at the @WestPoint_USMA or @AF_Academy 	- Midshipmen at the @NavalAcademy 	#DESTalks https://t.co/4dpcBTOi9u
Q6: Who is eligible for referral into the IDES? #DESTalks https://t.co/aruJTNEBue
A5: The IDES process is goaled to take 295 days for Active Duty members and 305 days for Reserve Component members to complete the process. Check out more information on DoD Policy, available here: https://t.co/U8EnWZYEKV #DESTalks https://t.co/A66bOND5UJ
Q5: How long can a Service member expect to be in the IDES? #DESTalks https://t.co/5Xoq1svXas
A4: In all cases, medical authorities will refer Service members for disability evaluation within one year of diagnosis. #DESTalks https://t.co/54wCf1duyj
@GIJaneret06 @DeptVetAffairs Thanks for your question, @GIJaneret06! The Service member's medical provider determines if and when a Service member is referred into the IDES based on their medical condition. Check out the answers to Questions 4&amp;6 coming shortly!
